 " vaise, sainya sahyog ke maamle main bharat ke liye america kii vah madad sabase zyaada mahatvapurn he, jo america use apana sabase bada vimanavahak pot banane main de rahaa he
 The United States has given the flight launch technology to India, which it itself is deploying in its aircraft ships, so that even larger fighter aircraft can fly from the ship itself
 isse bhartiya nausena ko takanic kii duniya main aage badhane main kaaphi madad milegi

 Significantly, India is the only one of the countries that have not signed the nuclear treaty, with which the US has made such a deal
 iske alaava agast maah main bhi narendra modi sarkaar ne ek logisticks samjhaute par dastakhat kiye the, jisase donon deshon ko ek-duusare ke sainya addon tak pahunch banane kii anumati mil gai he

 " america main republican party kii ore se raashtrapati pad ke pratyaashee donald trump kii 'america first' par aadhaarit videsh niti se jude bayanon ke maddenzar bharat tathaa anya asian deshon main atakalon kaa bazaar garm he ki trump ke jeetne kii sthiti main asia main america kii upasthiti kam kii ja sakati he

 unhone march maheene main 'neuyark times' ko die ek saakshaatkaar main kaha tha ki vah japan main bane beson se america fouj ko waapas bula sakate hai, or unhone is vichaar ko bhi hawa di thi ki vah japan or dakshin korea ko khud kaa parmaanu shastraagaar viksit karne de sakate hai

 unhone bataaya, "ek taraf trump kaa kahana he ki vah bharat ke saath vyapaarik sambandhon ko mahatv dete hai, lekin saath hi bhartiya kol centre main kaam karne waalon kaa mazaaq bhi udaate hai, or us pratiyogi maahaul kii andekhi karte hai, jo bharat ke saath sahyog karne par america ko hasil ho saktaa he
 
 
 Therefore, his views are not clear in a world where strong and mature diplomacy is needed
